forsaken lyckenes loue worldly thynges worldly man hath therfore exscused though stryue pursue goodes lawfull wayes haue hem ayen sayest thou behoueth haue thy necessaryes suche thynges longen well worldly man graunte well therto thou sholde loue self ne likyng haue holdyng ne ye kepyng ne sorowe ne heuynesse fele lesyng ye withdrawyng saynt gregory sayth asmoche sorow thou hast lesyng thinggreg moche loue haddest thou kepyng therfore yf thyn herte made hoole thou haddest sothfastly felt desire ghostly thynges wyth syghte leest ghostly thynge ye loue likyng ony erthly thynge thou sholdest sette noughte sholde cleue vpon loue haue nedeth skylfully oonly luste likynge grete defawte also fetchen thi loue vpon ye thinge nedeth selfe defawte soo grete haue vsen thyng nedeth wythoute loue kynde nede asketh wythoute whiche thyng maye vsed noo defawte othli poynte trowe many haue state lyknesse pouertee arn moche letted hyndered fro loue god ne accuse noo man ne noo state reproue eche astate arn good arn one thyng saye euery man woman hath taken state wylfull pouerte whether religyous seculer degree longe loue affeccyon bounden fastened glewed wyth ye loue ony erthly thing hath wolde haue may haue ne fele sothfastly clene loue clere syghte ghostly thynges aug saynt austyn sayd lorde thus lorde loueth lytill ye louyth ony thynge wyth loueth ye loue couetyse ony erthly thynge wyth lesse loue god thyn herte though loue erthly thyng putteth hem oute charite yf soo moche strangle loue god euen crysten sothely hyndreth hem letteth hem fro feruour charyte also fro speciall mede whiche shold haue blisse heuen perfite pouerte grete losse yf myghte see soo myght know ghostly mede good precyous worthy aye lastynge wolde loue erthly ioye hauour erthly thyng yf myghte haue wythoute syne lette ne lesse lest mede blysse heue whiche myghte haue yf wold speke ferther doo praye doo thus saye ye grace god thou maye ony man soo wyll comforte herte yf maye haue saye myghte haue ony creature whiche hath receyued plente grace see thenne syth couetyse naked grounde letteth man woman soo moche fro ghostly felyng loue god moche thene letteth combreth worldly men wymen whiche wyttes bodily besynes nyghte daye studye traueyle myghte gete ryches plente worldly good none delyte haue worldly thinges ne wyll seche say hem tyme wrytyng speke hem saye yf myghte see wolde see doo therfore thynkyth lykynge noo synne vnto saye yf thou kepe etynge drynkynge nedefull thynges thy body mesure thy nede thou receyuest noo likynge kynde askyth alle thou doost ghostely delite whiche thou felyst thy soule graute ye forsothe thou thenne synnest ryght nought therin thenne thou well ete slepe sothly wythouten doubte full ferre fro knowyng ferd fro werchynge ete haue kynde cune ete comyth vnd colour nede passyth nede lesse syne man synneth dedely comynly glotenye yf encombred wyth dedely synnes beforn done thene may lyght lyer synne dedely soth chesyth luste lykynge flesshe delayed full refourmyng mannes soule tyll laste ende saynt poul sayth deo pro nobis melius prouidente ne sine nobis consumarentur lorde purueyeth better v delaye refourmynge yf graunted thenne skylle chese god thene wretchydly felle hym sholde afterwarde refourmed sholde sette agayn free chesinge fyrst whether wolde haue profyte refourmynge noo maye skylle mane soule refourmed fully faste passyon refourmed fayth lycknesse god seconde reformyng puttyth oute likyng felynge flesshly stirynges worldly desyres suffreth noo suche spottes abyde ymage fyrste refourmynge oonly begynnyng profitynge felynges thorugh werkynge holy ghoste fyrste good seconde better thyrde blysse heuen moo beste fyrste lete v speke one syth soo shall come thyrde pthat thorugh sacrament baptym grounded passion cryste refourmed fro origynall synne caplm vi two maner synes makith soule lese ye shape lyknes god one called origynall yt firste syne thother called actuel yt wylfully done synne thyse ii synes put away soule fro ye blisse heue dapneth thendles payne helle yf thoruy grace god reformyd lyckenesse passe hen oute lyfe neuerthelesse two remedyes ayenst thise two synnes whiche forshapen soule maye refourmed lyckenesse god arn refourmed fayth arne refourmed fayth felynge thou shalt vnderstonde soule hath two partyes one called sensualyte flesshly felynge fyue outewarde wyttes whiche comon man
